## 1.0.0-beta.33.63.0 (2025-01-14)


### GET /api/team
-  added the required property `flags/forbidShareLinkCreation` to the response with the `200` status
-  added the required property `flags/requirePortalLogin` to the response with the `200` status


### PATCH /api/team/flags
-  added the new optional request property `forbidShareLinkCreation`
-  added the new optional request property `requirePortalLogin`
-  added the required property `forbidShareLinkCreation` to the response with the `200` status
-  added the required property `requirePortalLogin` to the response with the `200` status

## 1.0.0-beta.33.62.1 (2025-01-09)


### POST /api/workspaces/search
- ⚠️ the request property `filter/oneOf[subschema #1: WorkspaceSearchQueryFilterAnd]/inner` became required
- ⚠️ the request property `filter/oneOf[subschema #7: WorkspaceSearchQueryFilterOr -> subschema #6: WorkspaceSearchQueryFilterOr]/inner` became required
- ⚠️ removed `#/components/schemas/WorkspaceSearchQueryFilterMembersContainAny, #/components/schemas/WorkspaceSearchQueryFilterNameContain, #/components/schemas/WorkspaceSearchQueryFilterNameEqual, #/components/schemas/WorkspaceSearchQueryFilterNamespaceContainAny` from the `filter` request property `oneOf` list
-  added discriminator to `filter` request property
-  added `#/components/schemas/WorkspaceSearchQueryFilterMembers, #/components/schemas/WorkspaceSearchQueryFilterName, #/components/schemas/WorkspaceSearchQueryFilterNamespace` to the `filter` request property `oneOf` list




-  removed the schema `Property`
